6\. Me


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the avatar, you can fill in or edit your member information, such as mobile phone number, name, birthday, gender and other information. Click Confirm to submit, and the modifications are completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FGXEgNo85uviZKrKJKd7d%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd7c66a0&sv=2)

Click on the QR code icon. Your membership QR code will be displayed. With this membership QR code, you can show it to the terminal to recharge, identify membership, and other operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXDeGqK55knj76XMHXvfR%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31c84ebd&sv=2)

Click Me to enter my page, where you can see the user's own membership information, balance, points, membership coupons, membership codes, orders and other information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjV1zNuUQ97BUldJHM5vm%252F20.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae45c8bf&sv=2)

c4ba99daf639906596b582146927140

Click Balance to view your member's balance. Click Recharge Record to view the member's recharge record. You can select a time to view the recharge record for a specific date.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fo7XPQDbXh2vqs6uV0y8Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5daacad4-bce0-43a6-8eb1-cdccbed9c49f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ee6e128&sv=2)

Members can receive coupons after their purchase meets the amount set for the promotions. Next time when your purchase amount reaches a certain amount, you can use the coupon, the used coupon and Expired coupons will become invalid

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8u6r3brm0iGCp32qtZo4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D045d83be-bb2b-4626-80a6-dc177b23934b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c63183bb&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FgbzF0bqBhbtF8YsJqeGN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D980b2101-1f2b-4a4a-b228-5267d3b1806b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94a5c3ac&sv=2)

Click ALL in My Order to enter my order list and view orders with pending payment, pending shipment, picked up, and completed status.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FumhdKFJApc8fe1hCwqbt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46e26c88-14ca-41da-8946-0083c5de3663&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61dc3cb7&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfoYe8xAlnvkIwTmjXh2W%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ffd3b40-27f5-4737-8924-da25fb9f1b5f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1cd7943c&sv=2)

For unpaid orders, you can choose to cancel or pay. For orders that have been shipped, the customer can confirm receipt after receiving the goods and they will be converted into completed orders.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fxtj8Zs4B6UwFZYVisufc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df51650e5-4ed1-461b-9038-36e03f1764d7&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1ba97fc1&sv=2)

For completed orders, if you want to purchase again, you can click to view the details and place an order again.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FzammhfTAUPccTkTkwemL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D495cec37-c56d-464a-86d5-cae83eecbd0b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=132531d1&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F6xEHUmQ3zH50qxdztZJL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4174b58-df5a-4d9d-9e3c-df565c52ea31&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59d990cc&sv=2)

If you want to know the merchant's information, you can click Store profile to view the merchant's profile, and click Store address to view the merchant's address.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdrG8kvt4Msb4N23M4fJy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D368213de-9ab7-4312-b028-d97c52f5bcd5&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca118fe4&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F63dobqc0VBVpsYhLDsmd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f81d047-971a-4b7b-a3f2-c1357cf75589&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b9682a2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-online-store-user-guide#toc17650)

7\. Points Redeem


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On Me page, click Points to enter the redemption page of the points mall. The products and points redemption displayed here are set by the merchant portal. You can click Redeem to use existing points to redeem the product. Click Exchange Records, you can see the redeemed products, click to apply, a QR code will appear, and then use the terminal to scan and redeem.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQXQswOPhjj0k5KaTBCEh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2261f4e3-4a21-4f01-a320-4e32c14c7d33&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=acda0a66&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FE56Oehe3rJg46luVuGaw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D055fce85-b767-4625-a3e5-ab486073434e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b54b75a8&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FDAgnc9VMuPdmYRQGPrjm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De51bdbde-d833-4809-85dd-bbc55da262ea&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=56b65ca&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfdsI4oRMIdPk8WWTx018%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D058f8f4c-900f-4af1-a6a0-aa8cc10ac85c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=53bf6566&sv=2)

# UPT | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/upt#resources-in-wiki)

[Resources in Wikiarrow-up-right](https://sdkwiki.wizarpos.com/index.php?title=Payment_App)

*   Please choose the appropriate integration method based on your specific needs.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/upt#hardware)

Hardware

*   [UPT terminalsarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/techsupport/ticket/wizarpos_briefinfo.pdf)
    
*   [Serial Portsarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/techsupport/ticket/serialpicture.png)
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252Fzmf7COJJdvzulkT6BJxb%252Fserialpicture.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4408dd9-e5dc-49e5-9cd6-6347889c2f72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6316e59e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/upt#opc)

OPC

*   [Payment process flowchart for open-door cabinetsarrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/techsupport/ticket/opendoorpic.png)
    
*   The default timeout for OPC is 3 minutes. How can I set it to never time out?
    

Set paymentTimeout=0.

*   How do I change the logo at the bottom?
    

Set LogoUrl to the customized logo URL.

*   ProtocolType defination in OPC
    

DEFAULT: For calling AIDL API of OPC CLOUD MODE: use paywizard payment SERIAL SLAVE: use usb cable SERAL HOST: use UUcable MDB: use MDB SERIAL EXT: use physical serial port SERIAL EXT2: user RJ45 serial port PULSE MODE: use pulse SOCKET SERVER: use network

*   Why to set debug mode?
    

Only in debug Mode, can set payment app package name to the payment demo apk, other mode can not.

*   The default duration for debug mode is 5 days, which can be configured through parameter(keepDebugModeTime).
    
*   Enable exit directly: after set it, click Back button, will popup an Exit dialog, click Confirm button to exit it.
    
*   In OPC running page, long press the SN showed on the left-up corner, will popup a dialog, display the IP and the current Protocal Type.
    
*   The vending machine initiated the transaction, but it did not jump to the payment page. It is necessary to check if the payment package name has been configured correctly in OPC.
    
*   If the amount displayed in payment page is incorrect, please check the "currencycode" setting. If it is in MDB mode, please also check the "scaling factor" and "decimal places" settings.
    
*   Can I use two protocal modes? For example, use Default mode to do purchase, use cloud mode to do settlement?
    

No, you cann't, each mode will process through by OPC, in OPC, can only set one mode.

*   In cloud mode, what's the meaning of the "Unbound payment terminal"?
    

This is caused by the app hasn't bound the vending machine to the payment terminal yet.

*   When complete a pre-authorization, because different payment channels require different original transaction information, you can pass all the original transaction information defined in the protocol. Alternatively, you can add a check in your application and pass the original transaction information returned from the pre-authorization.
    
*   "connect payment app failed", when this error occured, please verify whether install payment app, then verify whether payment package name has set in OPC.
    
*   OPC call payment app, the default time out is 180s(3min), it can configure by paymentTimeout parameter.
    
*   CurrencyCode should transfer in each transaction.
    
*   How to obtain the serial number (SN) via OPC?
    

When making the protocol request, the value "SN" is passed in the AdditionalInfo field ("AdditionalInfo":"SN"). OPC will then return the device's serial number (SN) in the AdditionalInfo field of the response.

If develop app in terminal, please get SN by using android.os.Build.SERIAL

*   In the payment demo environment, using a bank card will not result in actual charges.
    
*   How to disable the user confirmation when payment?
    

Use the SkipConfirmProcedure parameter. It doesn’t wait for user confirmation and just proceeds automatically

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/upt#payment)

Payment

*   What parameters should be passed when canceling a pre-authorization? Is it TransIndexCode?
    

No, TransIndexCode is unique for each transaction, and its uniqueness is guaranteed by the third-party application itself, including transactions such as consumption, reversal, pre-authorization, pre-authorization incremention, and pre-authorization completion. For transactions requiring reversal, increment, or completion, the original transaction's TransIndexCode should be sent as OriTransIndexCode. Other original transaction data should be sent as Ori data: TraceNum->OriTraceNum, TransID->OriTransId, InvoiceNum->OriInvoiceNum, RRN->OriRrn.

*   How long does it take from the pre-authorization amount being authorized to the actual deduction?
    

Generally, it's real-time. Pre-authorization is a freeze, and pre-authorization completion is an unfreeze, which can be understood as a consumption transaction with real-time deduction. Pre-authorization and pre-authorization completion may not happen simultaneously. For example, when staying at a hotel, a pre-authorization of 500 yuan is made today, and tomorrow when leaving the hotel, the pre-authorization is completed for 400 yuan. The money is deducted when the pre-authorization is completed.

*   Canceling a pre-authorization:
    

TransType is Reversal

*   After sending a pre-authorization request message, if the user does not swipe the card after a certain period, it will return "cancel". If the card is swiped, a response will be received immediately.
    
*   Refund requires card swiping. However, in some versions of the refund process: if the order is already completed when sending the refund request, no card swiping is needed, and it will succeed immediately. If the order does not exist, it will wait for 1 minute and then return a timeout.
    
*   Reversal and pre-authorization completion do not require card swiping.
    
*   If a user spends two yuan, and we realize we made a mistake and need to refund 1 yuan
    

This scenario can be achieved by pre-authorizing 2 yuan and completing the pre-authorization for 1 yuan, or by consuming 2 yuan and reversing 1 yuan of the consumption.

*   Can Reversal only reverse pre-authorizations that have already been swiped, because there is a TransID in this case? If the user has not swiped the card, how should this pre-authorization be canceled?
    

You can use the protocol data CTRL: 0xC1 to indicate a Cancel Request.

*   After pre-authorization completion, no further additions can be made; it's equivalent to a completed deduction. Therefore, it's necessary to perform pre-authorization increment before the pre-authorization is completed; if you want to increase the deduction after completion, you must send a new pre-authorization and must swipe the card again, then pre-authorization completion; or send a card consumption transaction. Pre-authorization increment can be sent multiple times, but completion can only be sent once.
    
*   Settlement: Is it performed once a day at a specified time?
    

Yes.

*   When testing settlement, do we not need to send the amount? Should all unsettled transactions be automatically settled?
    

Yes, you don't need to send the amount.

*   Currency and minimum unit reference: [https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO\_4217arrow-up-right](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_4217)
    
*   The `transAmount` is always passed as an integer string. The actual amount depends on the minimum unit specified above. For example, if the unit is 2, then the amount will have two decimal places.
    
*   Can `refund` be called multiple times? For example, if 10 yuan was deducted, can it be refunded in three installments of 2, 6, and 2?
    

This is allowed for offline payments, but it depends on the specific payment channel. Most channels support this type of refund.

*   Generally, when we talk about scanning codes, we're looking at it from the user's perspective. When a user scans a POS terminal, it's a user-initiated scan; conversely, being scanned means the user's device is being scanned. 2c2p uses user-initiated scanning. QR code payment involves scanning the QR code on the mobile phone; it won't be displayed on the POS machine. The payment demo doesn't support user-initiated scanning because this demo is offline and doesn't have a backend to query payment results. Mpay currently only supports being scanned (passive scanning, where the merchant actively scans the payment code displayed on the consumer's mobile phone).
    
*   Are there any extra fees for refunds? Do you support partial refunds? What is the refund processing time?
    

Are there any extra fees for refunds? Do they support partial refunds? The refund processing time depends on the payment method and channel. Generally, there are no extra fees, and most methods support partial refunds. Refund times vary, ranging from instant processing to taking a day or up to 7 days, depending on the payment channel.

*   What is the maximum amount for a pre-authorization? How can a pre-authorization be canceled?
    

There is generally no upper limit set for the pre-authorization amount, but it usually does not exceed the maximum amount for a single transaction at the terminal (default is 999999.99). The pre-authorized amount can be released through a pre-authorization cancellation. If using OPC, this would involve calling the Reversal transaction.

*   Does a single POS terminal have a threshold for transactions awaiting settlement? If so, what is the threshold?
    

The settings for each channel are different, but generally the default is 500 transactions.

*   If a payment deduction or refund fails, is it possible to return the specific reason through the API?
    

Generally, a return code and return message will be returned.

*   Can a single pre-authorization be followed by multiple pre-authorization increment or pre-authorization completions (for example, due to insufficient funds or network issues causing transaction failure)?
    

This is also related to the payment channel; generally, one pre-authorization supports multiple subsequent transactions and is completed in a single process.

*   When settlement, will the uncompleted pre-authorization transactions be automatically captured?
    

No

*   if Purchased Amount > Pre-Auth Amount, then there will be a need to trigger a new sales transaction charge for remaining charge. Customer will need to tap the card again.
    
*   Once the pre-authorization is complete, no further amounts can be added. It's equivalent to a completed deduction. Therefore, any additions to the pre-authorized amount must be made before the pre-authorization is finalized. If you want to increase the deduction after completion, you will need to issue a new pre-authorization and complete the process again, requiring a card swipe; or you can process a separate card payment transaction.
    

[PreviousDisable Navigation Barchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/disable-navigation-bar)
[NextWizarview Open APIchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/wizarview-open-api)

Last updated 10 hours ago

# Retail Smart ECR User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

V1.2

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc22979)

1\. Function overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS Smart ECR retail app is a retail cashier system for Android big screen devices. It is used by cashiers in retail stores who use smart ECR machines to perform cashier operations on customers. The main functions provided by the system are as follows:

**1\. Goods**

Merchants upload various types of goods in the merchant portal and save all products in the product list. When customers shopping, the waiter scans the barcode of the goods to checkout.

**2\. Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts, special offers, points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can provide a better shopping experience.

**3\. Membership**

Each retail merchant can recommend the merchant's online store to the customer through links or QR code. Customers scan the QR code to register and become a member of the merchant. The staff can use the terminal to recharge the balance. The member's balance can be used at checkout. Members can receive coupons for consumption, which can be deducted when making purchases.

**4\. Payment**

Retail APP support cash, bank cards, membership cards, membership coupons and other payment methods.

**5\. Points**

Merchants can configure points redemption activities in the merchant portal, such as 100 points redeeming a bottle of Coke, 200 points redeeming a pack of snacks, etc. The waiter uses terminal to scan the customer's redemption code and redeem the product for the customer.

**6\. Chain stores**

If a merchant has multiple stores, it supports the chain store function. Customers can register as a member at any store under the merchant. The membership balance can be used across all stores. The membership coupons obtained through consumption can also be used at any store.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680710)

2\. Login


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the merchant number, user name, and password and click Login to enter the homepage.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0XEwpeGP7Gn7OXcm8NfC%252F0.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=276aaf64&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fc3iP3CJKP9jTcUVNRzFF%252F1.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2861ac9d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680711)

3\. Home


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The home page is the home page of the cashier, with a function bar at the top and various functions displayed on the left side of the function bar, such as selecting members, clearing the entire order, pending orders, and online store orders. On the right side are the product search function and operation panel (function aggregation bar), which displays all retail functions.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FcyadWoImDHdCAmtIbqVb%252F2.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=886958f&sv=2)

On this page, the cashier can use a scanner to scan the barcode of the product package and add the product to the product list. He or she can also select the product classification menu on the left to select the product to add to the product list. Of course, it also supports product search and purchase.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FxipmDncd1UNAcfxoOYMf%252F3.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c77579e5&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680712)

4\. Pending Order


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The cashier can temporarily suspend the items that are already in the pending order list, which is convenient for some customers who want to postpone the checkout, so that next customers can checkout first, and then select unchecked orders from the pending order list to perform checkout operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7hFQFr4bRQCnX36qgesQ%252F4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=146c3e81&sv=2)

Click on the pending order to place the item on hold.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FlXX5lH2PJPjyAXHJNIi8%252F5.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7840e36f&sv=2)

Click the left and right arrows under Actions to add items to your shopping cart and check out.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F8sKwpEFPGNGEPCKNnK2u%252F6.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca10cb08&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680713)

5\. Checkout


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Checkout in the lower right corner to enter the checkout page. The payment amount, taxes, discounts and other payment information are displayed on the left side of the page. The right side is the payment method. Customers can choose different methods to pay, such as cash, bank card, membership card, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fo6uRsZAKK90UCjMcQvbF%252F7.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c771c494&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrsSnVGwjF8Ge4jJnbeyP%252F8.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b85a56dd&sv=2)

On the home page, customers have several ways to identify themselves as members. First, customers can show their membership code QR code to the cashier, and the cashier can scan the QR code presented by the customer for identification. In addition, if necessary, the cashier can also manually enter the customer's membership code for binding. Once the binding is successful, the customer's membership information will be displayed in the upper left corner of the top.

At checkout, the system will display a membership card button, and customers can use their membership card balance to pay. In addition, the checkout function also supports the combination of different payment methods to pay multiple amounts, and coupons can also be used for deductions.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4h5aolJ1y81bp5vj06P6%252F9.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e09321f&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5Ev9SKDQ9PhvwrMnr0Te%252F10.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=537a1f94&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FwXd1OaNv1GEKOQ5brWx9%252F11.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37828e1c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680714)

6\. Online Orders


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the online store order above the checkout counter to enter the online store order page. You can view orders to be shipped, shipped, pending payment, completed, and canceled. Orders are divided into door-to-door delivery and self-pickup. You can enter for order details. For self-pickup orders, customers can show the delivery code and then scan the code to quickly locate the order and proceed with delivery. For shipped orders, you can view details and print the order receipt repeatedly.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fpg1SLRubot5HLtegClGT%252F12.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67d6c5be&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680715)

7\. Membership


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Member Query on the operation panel, enter the membership id or scan the membership QR code for member identification.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FI9xBe9axddLCu5zZjgVR%252F13.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=792d9a52&sv=2)

After the member is identified, enter the member management page. On this page, you can view the member's detailed information and recharge for the customer. In addition, members’ recharge records and consumption records can also be viewed on the page at any time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTOyuQbxdzNEn7lVQ0JuG%252F14.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce1ce241&sv=2)

Click Recharge, enter the recharge amount, and select the payment method to complete the recharge operation.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FgraRc3mBCYdDvSKvT1aK%252F15.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4a7e8b5&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FmincZl2Bnx2aF4R9PWk1%252F16.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dddcd066&sv=2)

Open the recharge record to query the member's recharge record.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FtsHDMp4XcTLar41QjQjN%252F17.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e9cdb68&sv=2)

Open the consumption record to query the member's consumption record.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7pvGMYJaGyKAmSaADQf3%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17d188f6&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680716)

8\. Goods Management


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the Product and Category button in the operation panel to enter the product management page. Click the category to select its product, and the product information will be displayed on the right. Click the lower right corner to modify or delete the product. You can also add new products under this category.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F2VNP3LxstphWjPQ7hS15%252F19.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c52a0df&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXY5mAcpx6hFKOViB6vvd%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c034eaa&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680717)

9\. Sales Order


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on the sales order in the operation panel to view the sales orders of all transactions. Click on one of the orders to view the order details and support refund operations. If the customer pays in cash, the merchant will refund the cash. If the customer pays with a membership card, the payment amount will be Automatically returned to the customer's membership card.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FThgIdXSHeN95NHPkPZxX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a1fdaa9-2743-45dc-8a57-b822a6d97373&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28f21aca&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FaJsiNgfi32ba9sfJLX7j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbb50083-e96f-48f3-ac44-8ad12840e39f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc966e8f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680718)

10\. Stock-in and Stock-out


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Stock-in and Stock-out in the operation panel to enter the merchandise inbound and outbound page. The page has functions such as warehousing, warehousing, warehousing records, and warehousing records.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FbG5IzzAvU19fsxK0PgVt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D296f8b3a-cef2-4292-8f28-898c4dd893cd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81332c9e&sv=2)

Click on the category of the product and select the product. You can fill in the quantity of the product on the right side. Click on the lower right corner to enter the warehouse. If the warehouse is successfully entered, click on the outbound warehouse to complete the outbound operation. You can also view the incoming and outgoing records.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FESJn1ijTOoNFPbJ2DIsd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3474c8b-1bb8-43f2-93b2-c166ad26cf53&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d474a413&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FZcYYmUEulPM5WTqbWNds%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f7faf8c-a2ad-4be8-b085-e7d3701a9532&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8381695&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FUA9XUtrduyGDbLwGkiOx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55851f43-c024-40b0-9e6a-2e5f8fe6c94d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e49a4abb&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680719)

11\. Inventory


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the inventory button in the operation panel to open the inventory page. Fill in the counted quantity according to the product, and display the profit and loss status.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLGIRLKQEEGCSqkTSqxbh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2774dfa0-469c-4790-b670-56e6790bfb46&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90e2b412&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680720)

12\. Business Report


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The business report can view the total sales amount of the day, full discounts and other information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FAfqiXLwoZGJi2E3Atmv6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f830c18-ea18-451e-bc22-e69da56d4595&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6a3f4a0&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680721)

13\. Stock Query


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Inventory inquiry can check the current quantity of goods in stock.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTYRY6c0I8QT8SJByWAgV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf40f129-56c1-4ea9-962a-026281b0abef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=30cfdf5b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680722)

14\. Points


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The points page displays the member's points redemption details, as well as the currently redeemed and pending items. The waiter can use the scanner function to scan the customer's point redemption QR code to redeem the items.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fp11FimlivuJ5UYkLyRQC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a9ec79d-b47a-46ee-bb98-a502b52c1315&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=293caf3b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143680723)

15\. Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the parameter setting page, you can configure printer parameters. Such as printer IP , print size, whether printing is enabled, etc.

# Set Agent Working Mode | CloudPOS SDK

1.  Access Terminal or Group Settings:
    
    *   In the TMS interface, navigate to 'Terminals > Terminal/Group'.
        
    
2.  Open System Parameter Configuration:
    
    *   Click on the 'Configure System Parameter' icon. This action will open the System Parameter page.
        
    
3.  Select the System Mode:
    
    *   On the System Parameter page, click on 'System'.
        
    *   Here, you can set the Agent Working Mode. There are four modes to choose from, 'Default' is also 'Full Function'.
        
    

Mode

Description

Data Usage

Full Function

Enables all functions of the Agent.

Approximately 5-10 MB per month, varying based on usage.

Standard

Major functions of the Agent are enabled.

Around 3-5 MB per month.

Low Traffic

Maintains the terminal online with minimal activity (heart beating). The terminal will not actively request the TMS server except for the first time after booting.

About 1-2 MB per month.

Ultra-low Traffic

Keeps the terminal online with very low frequency heartbeats, potentially causing delayed responses to TMS commands.

Less than 300 KB per month.

Note:

*   Choose the mode based on your data usage preferences and operational needs. Each mode balances functionality with data consumption, allowing you to optimize based on the specific requirements of your terminal network.
    

[PreviousPush APK to Specific Devicechevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apk-to-specific-device)
[NextManage APK Prompt Installationchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Retail Terminal APP User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc18639)

1\. Function Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS terminal retail app is a retail cashier system for Android terminal. It is used in retail stores. The main functions provided by the system are as follows:

**Goods**

Merchants upload various types of goods in the merchant portal and save all products in the product list. When customers shopping, the waiter scans the barcode of the goods to checkout.

**Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts, special offers, points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can provide a better shopping experience.

**Membership**

Each retail merchant can recommend the merchant's online store to the customer through links or QR code. Customers scan the QR code to register and become a member of the merchant. The staff can use the terminal to recharge the balance. The member's balance can be used at checkout. Members can receive coupons for consumption, which can be deducted when making purchases.

**Payment**

Retail APP support cash, bank cards, membership cards, membership coupons and other payment methods.

**Points**

Merchants can configure points redemption activities in the merchant portal, such as 100 points redeeming a bottle of Coke, 200 points redeeming a pack of snacks, etc. The waiter uses terminal to scan the customer's redemption code and redeem the product for the customer.

**Chain stores**

If a merchant has multiple stores, it supports the chain store function. Customers can register as a member at any store under the merchant. The membership balance can be used across all stores. The membership coupons obtained through consumption can also be used at any store.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc22756)

2\. Login


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please check the email of the merchant’s account. For accounts with operator roles, enter the merchant ID, username, and password to log in to the app. Check auto login will let you automatically log in next time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FaJF9d6xAhGsif7vZjbS3%252F0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=79f32a3&sv=2)

3\. Home


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The search bar allows you to search for products.

Scan function support 3 types of code:

1.Product barcode

2.Membership QR code

3.Pickup code

Stuff can place pending orders (unchecked orders are temporarily suspended), membership identify.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FejVjHhyqiM2QWntMAjGT%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39300553&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F3w1xVAZhpBTFrjLITm8W%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61b3a107&sv=2)

Click the Scan icon to scan the barcode of the product package with terminal and add it to the product list.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc20898)

4\. Pending Order


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The cashier can temporarily held the orders, for customers who want to postpone the checkout, so that the next customers can checkout first, and then select unchecked orders from the pending order list to perform checkout operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrwlkNtAn1QnGhbq5rmc6%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84d94c67&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FjpWMREA8FNUIzdxjELkU%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9750ce89&sv=2)

5\. Checkout


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Check out on the home page to enter the checkout page. You can use cash or bank cards to pay.

Identify Membership

The customer can present the membership QR code before checkout. The cashier clicks Membership to identify the membership, and the current member's info and balance will be displayed. At this time, the membership card icon and coupon icon will be available at checkout page. Checkout supports multiple payments with any payment method.

7\. Online Order


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Online order on the left menu to enter the mall order page. You can view the orders to be shipped, shipped, pending payment, completed, and canceled. The orders are divided into delivery and self-pickup. You can enter the order details. Click Delivery. For self-pickup orders, customers can show the delivery code, then scan the code to quickly locate the order and perform delivery operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLYCYlTwHXz05Mflm880B%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3735f9e5&sv=2)

For shipped orders, you can view details and reprint the order receipt.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F2OlqepumMPKSgs1fHGQ1%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b27e248&sv=2)

8\. Member


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Gift card on the left menu to enter the member identification page. You can identify members by scanning the QR code and entering the membership card number manually..

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FYDFTk6lcNAFqusbOdLOU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d65d32f-88e0-4cb8-8883-4ab7530608bd&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f703ce8&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfpMXlWLYUICMUJ2RvkLV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5175d946-b722-4aa1-bb72-5709ce359c68&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8763b43b&sv=2)

After the identification is successful, you can check the members info such as membership number, balance, and other information. Customer can recharge their membership card with cash or bank card. Also, can check the member's transaction history and the member's coupons.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fc6gsC2jZy7NkvUi5oIlv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e801117-bdcc-4bec-a6fc-40c660429d20&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17a6f14d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FBkWtanT9vXwQVYXSNvSH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d3b0288-8241-4907-b528-e32e13c7f7d1&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64f29d0c&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXWu6zpOgRNqPWqTxUn6C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0ba0b41-b1f6-4c13-a18d-84e92786f8dc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86fa29d0&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FXTTW8ekYfnp0JNL0nbNy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2f0098d-9c1b-4782-94cc-592b21736e4a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=793d3142&sv=2)

9\. Points Mall


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Points on the left menu to enter the points redemption function. Items currently redeemed and to be redeemed will be displayed. The cashier can use the scan function to scan the customer's points redemption QR code to redeem items.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQlc8sqwU5sCv0AjJzyKZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8917b380-ee31-433f-896e-554af9b3c5b6&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=af212af2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-retail/retail-terminal-app-user-guide#toc7772)

10\. Sales Report


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Sale report to enter the sales report, which displays the sales summary of the day. Click Print to print the report receipt.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdxomLdUCPVyvhUrh9jcR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9178880-8e06-4e4c-8975-9602df15044a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2634a698&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F7NOwxT5pLxv22NOIKKtJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa919f84-5770-4943-9839-82b53f69280d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1497cb9a&sv=2)

11\. Product Categories


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Goods & Categories to enter the category list. Click a category to enter the product list under that category. You can view product prices and de tails, add products, and edit and delete products.

Click + to add new products.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FalEcbw0F6MKceGIFE5aM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D062fa678-5b64-4e60-8505-e27a6c4193ab&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e38f1419&sv=2)

12\. Sales Order


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Sales Order to view all sales orders. Click on an order to view details. For sales orders, you can refund the order. After entering the manager password, you can perform refund operations.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQLL1jCV2wbsaDos8MFy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded53d234-8cc4-4467-98e8-98c5f5b6912d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5df9471&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrA2imSKwplu5KXBkVuqW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6692a5a-2a91-4331-98cb-001ac6de7dbf&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2551806&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FiduWdJXJLPg9qJqzYBgk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9194330b-1bf3-4abe-a4c2-897dcaef6256&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b74dff8&sv=2)

13\. Inventory Manage


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Inventory Manage to enter warehouse management.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fiu17U8oGB2780QeVribl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D842eaab5-181b-466a-bc4b-f1ac72e5c6dd&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31baf6c1&sv=2)

Click Stockin to enter the stock in process. You can scan the QR code and manually select the product. After confirming, the process is completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdoiIwnNSSedNAkIHSkej%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D179cdbbd-71fc-432a-9761-de2068772943&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=64980f3f&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCRKA0aNMZBzzTzQ23cuD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D172f2790-0a77-4c4a-aa05-cf952ab8702a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4368f970&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fw8HisZQBVaaIlT7Vq30l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D959d9141-06f9-4d7f-bfda-7df67571f81d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=41f3eb2&sv=2)

Click Stockout to enter the stock in process. You can scan the QR code and manually select the product. After confirming, the process is completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FYNI0JSipSAjkU0VUT6zi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9526459c-c15d-4384-8541-38947e0cbdee&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14da6d81&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FpvfK00HhhIc1Yijo1Cfl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe5279a4-6af7-4ea9-9287-d3804567b323&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73b09305&sv=2)

Click Inventory to enter the inventory count page. You can scan the QR code and manually select the product, then enter the inventory quantity of the product, and complete the count process.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FyYuGNgvAQf2JHNTbICEN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D721144df-092c-470d-99e7-6b626db96498&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e1e16eb&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fwkgh5mXDOM5IuELdAFkw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D778bb396-cd5d-4acb-a417-21d7a91ba177&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ba22875&sv=2)

Click Stock query to enter the inventory query.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FcQg7gUfzVdHU4x9qEo14%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29879079-36d2-4221-ba86-2110ac0387fc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=458dce3c&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FI3H0S1RwsWPbzn7H2Zc5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D36890d68-b204-483c-b50c-f5fd741b2abc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48c48b0e&sv=2)

Click Stockin query to enter the stockin query. The list displays all stockin orders. Select a stockin order to enter and query the stockin details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FimKPFcaCraLloLOk8h7O%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34e7e2e3-538e-4077-96bf-06f0e0ade02b&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d9962ba&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FGpkPPafesAGRyZMej61J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f5822ae-ad64-4960-b6a7-e50d2a03196c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efab1c7d&sv=2)

Click Stockout query to enter the stockout query. The list displays all stockout orders. Select a certain stockout order to enter and query the stockout details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FJKYPIGYpNAmGhOu610TV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ee7a797-2bb7-49b0-8959-dac618c62c31&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=af5a8d5d&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FFJ0FitQRwxlTwcdyOwku%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bfc6d5d-9f3c-4069-918f-6188a4e45428&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2c8b643&sv=2)

Click Inventory query to enter the inventory query and display all inventory orders. Click to view the details of a certain inventory order. You can also filter the inventory orders within a certain time period based on time to view.

14\. Parameter settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the parameter setting page, you can view the quantity of the current order receipt. You can turn on/off message notifications. After turning it on, the order placed by the customer in the mall will be notified to the handheld retail store. You can clear the cache and data below.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0SC4ONn3COZmj2IH6QZC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D598bc107-1887-4e54-a85b-4c3e2d3c0e0f&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2da0ba4&sv=2)

# Push APK to Specific Device | CloudPOS SDK

1.  Navigate to Application Management:
    
    *   In the TMS interface, go to 'Applications > Application'.
        
    
2.  Add or Update an App:
    
    *   Choose to either add a new app or update an existing one. This action will open the application page.
        
    *   Confirm 'Group' and 'Name'.
        
    
3.  Access Advanced Options:
    
    *   On the application page, click the 'Advance' icon to view more configuration options.
        
    
4.  Define Target Device Serial Number (SN):
    
    *   Click the 'Search' icon in the 'Target SN' field. This will open the 'Choose Terminal Model' page.
        
    *   The 'Target SN' field supports regular expressions. By using a regular expression, you can select serial numbers that match the specified pattern.
        
    
5.  Select the Device Type:
    
    *   Select the specific device type, then click 'Commit".
        
    
6.  Configure the App to a Group:
    
    *   The app should be configured to a group. This ensures that the APK is only pushed to terminals within that group that match the selected device type.
        
    

Note:

*   It’s important to use the correct regular expression in the 'Target SN' field to accurately target the desired devices.
    
*   Ensure that the group configuration is correctly set up to include only the intended device types.
    

[PreviousUpdate Firmware Remotelychevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/update-firmware-remotely)
[NextSet Agent Working Modechevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/set-agent-working-mode)
