# Catering Smart ECR User Guide | WizarPOS Catering & Retail Soloution User Guide

WizarPOS Catering Solution

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508823)

1\. Function Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WizarPOS Smart ECR Catering is a professional ordering system based on Android devices, providing efficient services and convenient ordering experience to catering merchants. The system has the following functions:

**1\. Menu**

The merchant uploads various types of dishes, hot dishes, cold dishes, Western food, dim sum, snacks, etc. And displays all the dishes in the menu. When ordering, the dishes can be customized according to the specifications, tastes, methods, and toppings.

**2\. Promotions**

Merchants can set up various types of marketing activities through the merchant portal, including discounts, full discounts, special offers, points malls, coupons for consumption and other activities, which can provide great dining experiences.

**3\. Membership**

Each catering merchant can use the table QR code or takeout QR code to allow customers to scan the QR to register and become a member of the merchant. The waiter can use terminal to recharge for the members, and the member balance can be used when order and pay. Members can get coupons through consumption.

**4\. Payment**

Handheld ordering can support cash, bank cards, membership payment, membership coupons and other payment methods.

**5\. Points**

Merchants can configure goods for exchange in the merchant portal, such as 100 points to exchange for a bottle of Coke, 500 points to exchange for a dish. The waiter uses a terminal to scan the customer's redemption code and redeem the goods for the customer.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508824)

2\. Login


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to log in to the terminal, you need to enter the merchant ID, username and password.

The merchant ID is when the service provider onboarding the merchant. An assigned merchant ID can be obtained from the email after the merchant is successfully onboarded. At the same time, the merchant administrator account and initial password will be given. The merchant administrator must log in to the merchant backend for the first time, change the initial password, and create an operator account in System Settings -> Account Management. The created operator account can be used to log in to the terminal catering application.

**Note:** **The administrator account of the merchant received by email cannot be used to log in to the terminal application.**

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FfTx0rK0jd1SV4HHICf3l%252F0.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4da7a91&sv=2)

Enter the MID, username, and password, and click Login to enter the homepage.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FTY5zLG7yuxLpHg1PmAog%252F1.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69df1a30&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508825)

3\. Home


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The home page is divided into three areas, function area on the left, display area in the middle, and the checkout area below.

The function area has the following functions:

Dine-in, reservations, reports, membership, points, takeout, notifications, menu management and settings.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FX1KpWMpYAg3aVWCxFla6%252F2.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afedd7c1&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508826)

4\. Dine-in


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The merchant clicks on the dine-in to choose the table, and the table displays the table name, maximum customer and status. The table status is divided into free and dining. The table is set in the merchant portal. Click the table to enter the menu.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FOmTBcEQ0dAIvQtkTfVvX%252F3.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=655f41db&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FdjyIrhPHU4ARJSvMqHfj%252F4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=286dd5ec&sv=2)

In the menu, you can select dishes according to the category of the dishes, and you can choose the specifications, tastes, toppings, and methods of the dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Flz2R29CQBOGcX10MkgWK%252F5.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e668761a&sv=2)

Select dishes and dish specifications to add to the ordering list on the right. You can view the selected dishes in the ordering list, and support modify dishes. Click Remarks below to fill in the remark information.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FLgAm26m4hshMDPykePk5%252F6.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65c5d7cc&sv=2)

Click Order to place an order. The table status changes to dining, the printer print receipts and kitchen receipts, and the kitchen prepares dishes according to the order.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F5B826E47zOp9QtUJv0zZ%252F7.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db3e2381&sv=2)

Select the table and click the dining button on the lower right to jump to the ordering list. On this page, waiter can modify dishes .

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F3mtXMRQBoTUucJRSkFcW%252F8.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d9d4cc9&sv=2)

Select the dining table and click the bill button to jump to the payment. The cashier displays the payment amount, taxes, discount information on the total order amount, etc. You can choose the payment method, such as split payment (multiple payments), and the customer selects the tip ratio or directly enters the tip amount.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fw8USFIPnfLM4RchTqLXo%252F9.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc4e09d0&sv=2)

Click on the number of people to split the order, up to 10 orders; click on the tipping ratio, the default is 10%, 15%, 20%, which can also be customized in the system settings.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FckU5SG5Izf5Fv4kYz8l0%252F10.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c895f85d&sv=2)

Payment methods include cash payment, bank card payment, membership payment or other payment. Among them, bank cards need to be connected to payment channels, and membership payments need to identify membership QR code. Click on the lower right corner for member identification.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FoG6B0yhUoo9jTm6d5Akx%252F11.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e07b8a60&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FPWvRlZ0Xu0jNCacLeLJK%252F12.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b43e34a7&sv=2)

After identifying the member, you can choose a membership card or coupon to pay. You can also use other payment methods customized by the merchant to record other types of transactions.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FQBCo8YFFWVu1dO6toAyr%252F13.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96b7a44&sv=2)

After a success payment, you will be redirected to the home page, the table will be changed to idle, and the label machine will print the receipt.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrxVY12xegAZRyMsUrNSG%252F14.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e94f2a05&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508827)

5\. Reservations


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click Book to enter the table reservation list. The page can manage customers' reservation table information. Make reservations for customers based on table. Reservation information includes date, reservation time, number of diners, etc.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FrWQQBfZa9zcX2FY3hKly%252F15.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88990721&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508828)

6\. Reports


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the report menu, and the page displays business reports, sales orders, today's summary and tip reports. These reports are summary queries that can query order information based on time period and type.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508829)

6.1 Sales Reports

The business report displays the revenue, discounts, refunds and other information of the day's business, and supports printing of business report documents.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FS9qLWUejIWnrKjzbubix%252F16.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c3f7fe5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508830)

6.2 Sales Order

Sales reports can query order details based on time range and type.

Sales Orders display all online and dine-in orders.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEBEnYXVV0deh8CLW9imQ%252F17.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3938081&sv=2)

Select an order and click to view details. In the pop-up window, you can view all the details of the order, and you can print or return the order. Refund requires entering the manager password, which is set in the merchant's portal.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FmOYrK0IeDZjO4PpQ94eR%252F18.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee37ede8&sv=2)

After entering the password to perform the refund operation, a refund receipt will be printed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0KbteBPU1u6YMEIIltvU%252F19.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a5c7d96&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508831)

6.3 Today’s Summary

You can view all the dishes sold today on today's summary page.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEJOJAy502qBlv7DI0oZE%252F20.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40ee55d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508832)

6.4 Tip Report

Click Tips Report to enter tip statistics. You can check the tip amount and number of orders based on employees and time.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F0RqTmlhvjzupGT7aUnly%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1465079e-1ac6-4eaa-b771-2be6a7433992&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=23810904&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508833)

7\. Membership


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the member menu to enter the member inquiry page. You can enter the member ID or scan the QR code. After identifying the member, its balance, number of points, and number of coupons will be displayed. You can recharge for the members, and you can also view recharge details and transaction details.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F31wXy6NYqx3wM8JFPgnq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5740209-b8d7-4bc0-b921-107c94d8e1d1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10959a34&sv=2)

Click Recharge to enter the recharge page. The payment method supports cash and bank card. Enter the recharge amount. After the payment is successful, the balance will be credited immediately. Member accounts can also view coupons.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F40cENA1T1k7ei5h3zrQa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e1c9af4-1f19-4776-bcac-e1d81e043ba6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2a58a57&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FNC3YUJcbw25A0HMIjB9k%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3865f0ed-cfa3-4e43-a302-caa078c45368&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b7b3cdc&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FDtQOvg7t2rx2fi5Ihn1j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd86c694-a2f1-4abc-970a-a65fe53b7b4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3829ac68&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508834)

8\. Points


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the points menu to enter the points redemption function. The page displays the redemption records, including items used and to be used. The waiter can use the scanner to scan the customer's points redemption QR code to redeem items.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fdu4akabzKHIfY4wNg4U8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8b677fa-3c80-4993-a733-f24099560ac2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13e9eca9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508835)

9\. Delivery


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on Delivery to enter the takeout list. The page displays two lists of picked up and unpicked meals. Select the unpicked meal list, click on the order and click on the lower right corner to pick up the meal, then the status of the order will change to Completed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F4MCvqKU09VM153RXH4JC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbba05c0c-ce92-4419-8aaa-b863d690e2b7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61f06c6a&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508836)

10\. Queue


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the queuing page. On the page, you can check the queuing status of the table, such as the number of people at the table, waiting time, etc. The waiter can click the three icons in the list to perform voice announcements, customer dining and queuing invalidation. Click on the number transfer information at the bottom right to view the historical queue details that have expired.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F1BflCb6XkfewxZLEtLIT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D107ee1be-2cd1-45d3-a36a-6e9d77ae412c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=847efca3&sv=2)

Click the pick up number button, select the type of the table, and the terminal will print a receipt to the customer. Customers can use their mobile phone browser to scan the QR code on the ticket to check the queue information in real time to prevent passing the number.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252F2gcKLGUJyDkjMcxUeigQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1fbabe79-8239-4be1-a5c3-58e18eaf6d9c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f01dd9f&sv=2)

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FeglOuOixjCZSXl6jLAmP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d52cb49-c085-4a01-ac6d-5cfd935f0557&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b20e6f4e&sv=2)

After scanning the QR code, check the current dining queue status on your mobile browser.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fm1bPzOuXfFcYqlqMYiL6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D429e2fdc-7bf1-4025-a9f4-e47ee2dbe7cb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=560eee6f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508837)

11\. Menu Management


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The menu management page supports the operations of adding, modifying, and deleting dishes. You can modify the sold out status of a dish.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FEdJaxfB75JMnIcgZRHwn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D643ad5a7-a2c2-4cb3-bdd9-83c485465e24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cebdd44d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508838)

12\. Category Management


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In category management, you can create categories for dishes to make it easier to manage dishes.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FHiGLV2KKdEUr9GF2oWgQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded9b0bda-6a72-45e6-9042-4e78b0d602f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf36b094&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508839)

13\. Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the settings menu to enter the system settings page, which displays basic parameters, printing parameters, and other payment settings. The basic parameters display relevant information such as the current merchant number and merchant name. You can turn on or off the message notification function as needed, and choose whether to automatically receive orders. By default, these two functions are turned off. When turned off, you need to manually receive orders and print operations. When turned on, the terminal will automatically print new orders. Merchants can also set different tip ratios according to needs.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FCGVZqjPrDwcFlpVnIigs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f772d03-6be8-4022-8a57-07c9f0187043&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19a97153&sv=2)

In the printing parameters, you can configure the parameters related to the back kitchen and front desk cashier printing.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252FJhVFEqcLUFiPoEsGDs3t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac56efc3-5371-4b12-888d-0a6894288c30&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26895001&sv=2)

Other payments are to configure payment methods other than mainstream payment methods.

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/product-user-guides/smart-catering/catering-smart-ecr-user-guide#toc143508840)

14\. Notification


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the notification menu, you can receive order notifications for customers' online orders on their mobile phones. The green icon represents a dine-in order. If a customer places an order but does not pay, they will receive a corresponding order notification and the waiter can click to take the order and print it. The yellow icon represents a takeout order. After the customer places the order and completes the payment, the order notification will be received in the message notification bar, and the waiter can click to take the order and print it. If the kitchen network printer has been configured , the kitchen receipt will be automatically printed.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/wizarpos-catering-and-retail-soloution-user-guide/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1012038583-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F6WUxwQSQcDz5p25hG7s0%252Fuploads%252Fuk2sgyxJSerpZYcuH5GX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b62251e-f53b-411f-a4d2-6af85ca46d72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8494e039&sv=2)

# Understand Agent Error Codes | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#error-format-overview)

Error Format Overview

Errors in the TMS and the agent are formatted as follows:

*   '\[L/LS/S\]-\[module code\]-\[error code\]'
    
*   Example: 'L\_01\_28'
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#error-prefix-explanation)

Error Prefix Explanation

*   'L': Indicates a general error originating from the terminal.
    
*   'LS': Denotes a network-related error from the terminal.
    
*   'S': Represents a general error from the WizarView server.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#module-code)

Module code

This part of the error code specifies the module in the system where the error occurred. (Details of module codes should be listed here.)

*   01: Adapt agent parameter
    
*   02: Adapt device parameter
    
*   03: Adapt network parameter
    
*   04: Reset administrator password
    
*   05: Uninstall app from terminal
    
*   06: Update app
    
*   07: Update communication key
    
*   08: Upload app status
    
*   09: Upload app parameter status
    
*   10: Upload system event
    
*   11: Upload app which terminal has installed
    
*   12: Upload log
    
*   13: Terminal register
    
*   14: Upload error log when turn on terminal
    
*   15: Update firmware patch
    
*   16: Update Unionpay key
    
*   17: Upload app info
    
*   A: Administrator login
    
*   B: Administrator logout
    
*   C: Task when turn on terminal
    
*   D: Modify Administrator password
    
*   DT: Download App/firmware/parameter file
    
*   E: Mount SD Card
    
*   F: Collect system event
    
*   G: Tip message of install firmware
    
*   H: Install app
    
*   I: Install parameter file
    
*   J: Install firmware
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#error-code)

Error code

The error code is a specific identifier for the type of error. (A list of common error codes should be provided here.)

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#for-l)

For L

*   0: Network error
    
*   999: Unknown error
    
*   10: Install app error
    
*   11: Uninstall app error
    
*   12: Install parameter error
    
*   13: Install firmware error
    
*   14: Register address can not access
    
*   15: Input register address is same with the default register address
    
*   16: Communication key message parsing error
    
*   17: Can not identify the message from WizarView
    
*   18: Verify signature fail by certificate
    
*   19: Verify signature fail by communication key
    
*   20: HSM error, generate CSR fail
    
*   21: HSM error, encrypt data fail
    
*   22: Terminal has registered
    
*   23: File I/O error
    
*   24: Download app error
    
*   25: Operation running
    
*   26: File is not exist
    
*   27: Can not find the app
    
*   28: Return fail when call interface
    
*   29: The interface is not exist
    
*   30: Verify administrator password fail
    
*   31: Can not identify file format
    
*   32: Can not parse command from WizarView
    
*   33: Illegal message from WizarView
    
*   34: Customer serial number is null
    
*   35: Firmware has existed
    
*   36: Download module are working
    
*   37: Terminal does not register
    
*   38: System event monitor initialize fail
    
*   39: Public certificate lost from HSM
    
*   40: Encrypt fail from HSM
    
*   41: HSM does not initialize
    
*   42: SN is not exist
    
*   43: Mount SD card fail
    
*   44: Terminal initialize fail
    
*   45: Have not connected network
    
*   46: Download fail, unknown reason
    
*   47: Download fail, please check from terminal
    
*   48: Can not connect to WizarView
    
*   49: Terminal is initializing
    
*   50: No permission
    
*   \-888: Parameter error
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#for-s)

For S

*   0:Close reqAppList or Firmware version name don‘t match regex
    
*   2:Sn is null
    
*   3:Invalid csr
    
*   4:Xmpp password of login is empty
    
*   5:Communication cert lost
    
*   6:Communication cert changed
    
*   707:Sn does not exist
    
*   705:Communication cert lost
    
*   709:Verify signature fail by cert
    
*   710:Verify signature fail by key
    
*   8:Terminal has none certificate
    
*   11:Add openfire user fail or Add MQTT user fail
    
*   12:Not define register rule
    
*   13:No matched register rule
    
*   14:Generate cert error
    
*   15:Pinpad key changed
    
*   16:Pinpad key lost
    
*   17:Communication key lost
    
*   18:Not define signature type
    
*   20:Request not supported
    
*   25:Obtaining sn key
    
*   26:Sn Key and package name no changed
    
*   27:Terminal has no sn key.
    
*   28:Can not obtain sn key
    
*   29:No firmware is configured!
    
*   30:Add firmware patch task success
    
*   31:Patching task is added
    
*   32:Patch is already exists
    
*   33:Add patching task failed
    
*   34:Old firmware version does not exist
    
*   35:New firmware version does not exist
    
*   36:Execute external command failed
    
*   37:Upload patch to wizarview failed
    
*   38:Calculate patch failed
    
*   39:No matched terminal model
    
*   40:The NEW group lost
    
*   48:The firmware is already the latest version
    
*   50:certificate is not exist
    
*   51:request sig error
    
*   52:request sig failed whth unknown exception
    
*   53:Unknown pakcage name or label
    
*   54:The terminal kernel type isn't match with target firmware
    
*   55:The transfer code is not found
    
*   56:The transfer code is expired
    
*   57:The transfer code is invalid - User is locked
    
*   58:The transfer code is invalid - User is closed
    
*   59:The terminal model type isn''t match with target firmware.
    
*   60:The terminal lock rule is unchanged
    
*   61:The agent need upgrade
    
*   62:The terminal system customer type isn't match with target firmware
    
*   65:Regsiter message need signature
    
*   66:Invalid register certificate
    
*   67:Invalid register signature
    
*   68:Sig message error on server
    
*   70:Soft sim - no device with imei
    
*   71:Soft sim lack imei or flow param
    
*   72:Soft sim no order on device
    
*   73:No remote control service available
    
*   74:Firmware model not match
    
*   75:Softsim service error
    
*   80:Terminal not visible
    
*   81:The firmware patch is disabled
    
*   82:The firmware patch message version lost
    
*   83:Lost pakcage name
    
*   84:Lost app name
    
*   85:Invalid JSON data
    
*   86:Upload application log setting is not available
    
*   87:The upload application log request is missing parameters
    
*   1012:Terminal has binding with app
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#for-ls)

For LS

*   400: Bad request
    
*   403: Forbidden
    
*   404: Not found the resource
    
*   500: Internal server error
    
*   503: Bad gateway
    
*   504: Gateway timeout
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/understand-agent-error-codes#common-error-codes)

Common error codes

List out the common error codes, their meanings. This part is crucial for users to understand what each error code signifies.

Error Message

Description

999

The terminal failed to register due to unknown reasons, please click Update Now.

L\_12\_33

Server message is illegal

L\_13\_06

Terminal certificate conflict

L\_13\_20

CSR failed to generate

L\_15\_13(29)

Update firmware patch failed because because the interface is not exist the API version needs update. BAD\_API\_VERSION = 29.

L\_I\_12(27)

Apk is not installed according to the package name. PACKAGE\_OR\_APPINFO\_NOT\_FOUND = 27.

L\_I\_13

Install Firmware failed because an unexpected exception. INSTALL\_FIRMWARE\_FAILED = 13.

L\_I\_13(29)

Install Firmware failed because the interface is not exist the API version needs update. BAD\_API\_VERSION = 29.

L\_I\_28

Install Firmware failed because returning fail when call interface. INVOKE\_ADDITIONAL\_API\_FAILED = 28.

L\_IA\_10(-1)

Install apk failed because the package is already installed. INSTALL\_FAILED\_ALREADY\_EXISTS = -1.

L\_IA\_10(-2)

The package archive file is invalid. INSTALL\_FAILED\_INVALID\_APK = -2.

L\_IA\_10(-3)

Install apk failed because the URI passed in is invalid. INSTALL\_FAILED\_INVALID\_URI = -3.

L\_IA\_10(-4)

Install apk failed because the package manager service found that the device didn't have enough storage space to install the app. INSTALL\_FAILED\_INSUFFICIENT\_STORAGE = -4.

L\_IA\_10(-5)

Install apk failed because the package is already installed with the same name. INSTALL\_FAILED\_DUPLICATE\_PACKAGE = -5.

L\_IA\_10(-6)

Install apk failed because the requested shared user does not exist. INSTALL\_FAILED\_NO\_SHARED\_USER = -6.

L\_IA\_10(-7)

Installed package has a different signature than the new package. INSTALL\_FAILED\_UPDATE\_INCOMPATIBLE = -7.

L\_IA\_10(-8)

Install apk failed because the package is requested a shared user which is already installed on the device and does not have matching signature. INSTALL\_FAILED\_SHARED\_USER\_INCOMPATIBLE = -8.

L\_IA\_10(-9)

The new package uses a shared library that is not available. INSTALL\_FAILED\_MISSING\_SHARED\_LIBRARY = -9.

L\_IA\_10(-10)

Install apk failed because the package uses a shared library that is not available. INSTALL\_FAILED\_REPLACE\_COULDNT\_DELETE = -10.

L\_IA\_10(-11)

Install apk failed because the package failed while optimizing and validating its dex files, either because there was not enough storage or the validation failed. INSTALL\_FAILED\_DEXOPT = -11.

L\_IA\_10(-12)

Can't install because the current SDK version is older than that required by the package. INSTALL\_FAILED\_OLDER\_SDK= -12.

L\_IA\_10(-13)

Can't install because provider name is already used by other apk. INSTALL\_FAILED\_CONFLICTING\_PROVIDER= -13.

L\_IA\_10(-14)

Install apk failed because the package failed because the current SDK version is newer than that required by the package. INSTALL\_FAILED\_NEWER\_SDK = -14.

L\_IA\_10(-15)

Install package failed because it is a test-only package. INSTALL\_FAILED\_TEST\_ONLY = -15.

L\_IA\_10(-16)

Install apk failed because the package being installed contains native code, but none that is compatible with the the device's CPU\_ABI. INSTALL\_FAILED\_CPU\_ABI\_INCOMPATIBLE = -16.

L\_IA\_10(-17)

Install apk failed because the package uses a feature that is not available. INSTALL\_FAILED\_MISSING\_FEATURE = -17.

L\_IA\_10(-18)

Install apk failed because a secure container mount point couldn't be accessed on external media. INSTALL\_FAILED\_CONTAINER\_ERROR = -18.

L\_IA\_10(-19)

Install apk failed because the package couldn't be installed in the specified install location. INSTALL\_FAILED\_INVALID\_INSTALL\_LOCATION = -19.

L\_IA\_10(-20)

Install apk failed because the media is not available. INSTALL\_FAILED\_MEDIA\_UNAVAILABLE = -20.

L\_IA\_10(-21)

Install apk failed because the verification timed out. INSTALL\_FAILED\_VERIFICATION\_TIMEOUT = -21.

L\_IA\_10(-22)

Install apk failed because the verification did not succeed. INSTALL\_FAILED\_VERIFICATION\_FAILURE = -22.

L\_IA\_10(-23)

Install apk failed because the package changed from what the calling program expected. INSTALL\_FAILED\_PACKAGE\_CHANGED = -23.

L\_IA\_10(-24)

Install apk failed because the package is assigned a different UID than it previously held. INSTALL\_FAILED\_UID\_CHANGED = -24.

L\_IA\_10(-25)

Install apk failed because WizarView apk version is lower than terminal used apk version

L\_IA\_10(-26)

Install apk failed because the package has target SDK low enough to not support runtime permissions. INSTALL\_FAILED\_PERMISSION\_MODEL\_DOWNGRADE = -26.

L\_IA\_10(-100)

Install apk failed because the package does not end with the expected '.apk' extension. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_NOT\_APK = -100.

L\_IA\_10(-101)

Install apk failed because the package is unable to retrieve the AndroidManifest.xml file. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_BAD\_MANIFEST = -101.

L\_IA\_10(-102)

Install apk failed because the package encountered an unexpected exception. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_UNEXPECTED\_EXCEPTION = -102.

L\_IA\_10(-103)

Did not find any certificates in the .apk. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_NO\_CERTIFICATES = -103. Maybe developer sign the apk with wrong signature format, e.g. Q2 does not support signature format v2.

L\_IA\_10(-104)

Inconsistent certificates on the files in the .apk. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_INCONSISTENT\_CERTIFICATES = -104.

L\_IA\_10(-105)

Install apk failed because the package encountered a CertificateEncodingException in one of the files in the .apk. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_CERTIFICATE\_ENCODING = -105.

L\_IA\_10(-106)

Install apk failed because the package encountered a bad or missing package name in the manifest. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_BAD\_PACKAGE\_NAME = -106.

L\_IA\_10(-107)

Install apk failed because the package encountered a bad shared user id name in the manifest. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_BAD\_SHARED\_USER\_ID = -107.

L\_IA\_10(-108)

Install apk failed because the package encountered some structural problem in the manifest. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_MANIFEST\_MALFORMED = -108.

L\_IA\_10(-109)

Install apk failed because the package does not find any actionable tags (instrumentation or application) in the manifest. INSTALL\_PARSE\_FAILED\_MANIFEST\_EMPTY = -109.

L\_IA\_10(-110)

Install apk failed because the system failed to install the package because of system issues. INSTALL\_FAILED\_INTERNAL\_ERROR = -110.

L\_IA\_10(-111)

Install apk failed because WizarView apk version is lower than terminal used apk version. INSTALL\_FAILED\_VERSION\_DOWNGRADE = -111.

L\_IA\_10(-112)

Install apk failed because the package doesn't have a native library for terminal cpu architecture. INSTALL\_FAILED\_NO\_MATCHING\_ABIS = -112.

L\_IA\_10(-1000000)

Install apk failed because a reason undefined so far. INSTALL\_FAILED\_OTHER = -1000000. If agent version is lower than 5239, \[L\_IA\_10(-112)\] is included.

L\_IA\_13(66)

Firmware installation service execution failed. POSSYS\_UNZIP\_FAIL = 66.

LS\_XX\_49

Can't connect to wizarView due to network problem.

LS\_13\_0

WizarView server has unknown error.

L\_DT\_47

The terminal can not access download server, because of local network problem or download server is down.

# Update Firmware Remotely | CloudPOS SDK

Updating firmware remotely for terminals can be accomplished in three different ways. Each method has its own advantages and considerations.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/update-firmware-remotely#update-with-full-firmware-package)

Update with Full Firmware Package

*   Description: This involves downloading the entire firmware package from the vendor. Example file name: '2023xxxx-Q3A7-wizarpos-TF-Sxxxx-mid-user-nosplash.zip'.
    
*   Considerations:
    
    *   The full package is usually large, around 500MB, so a stable Wi-Fi or Ethernet connection is recommended for the update.
        
    *   Ensure sufficient internal storage on the terminal, as lack of space could lead to update failure.
        
    *   This method is less recommended due to its size and the potential for storage issues.
        
    
*   Procedure: Obtain the package from the vendor and configure it in TMS as an Application with the type ‘firmware’. Do not unzip the file before configuration
    
*   Create application of firmware type
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252F7QsFM3YXP2OJd4mESh4K%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7680631-d501-426e-9cfc-ab65d67eafd0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4fadd5be&sv=2)

*   Choose the firmware application
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FzknNdKQWw4Xnv2GWDbRa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee6b3699-8782-48d5-b0fe-e4ba1295f429&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=993cda63&sv=2)

*   Firmware version list
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FMjMbxBf3XZyCPwsy7dRB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e8795a5-752c-4521-aae3-17527a874108&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61e7871b&sv=2)

*   Firmware upload
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252F34NA8kGsFpZYgfZE28a6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db34ecd96-b199-4c9c-a7bf-9c2623744ab1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bfffd58a&sv=2)

*   Configure the firmware to terminals or groups
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252Fxma7VO15o4L9kF8cm0Aq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b103a15-f3bb-4d78-9075-736702191546&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=62e34875&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/update-firmware-remotely#update-with-specific-firmware-patch-package)

Update with Specific Firmware Patch Package

*   Description: A firmware patch is a smaller update tailored to a specific old firmware version of the terminal.
    
*   Considerations:
    
    *   The patch is typically less than 100MB.
        
    *   Be cautious to match the patch package with the correct old firmware version to avoid errors.
        
    
*   Procedure: Obtain the specific firmware patch package from the vendor and configure it in WizarView as an Application with the type ‘firmware’.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/update-firmware-remotely#update-with-auto-generate-patch-package)

Update with Auto-Generate Patch Package

*   Description: An advanced option where the vendor configures a target firmware version for your terminal.
    
*   Considerations:
    
    *   Patch packages generated are usually under 100MB.
        
    *   TMS automatically generates the necessary patch, eliminating the need to consider the old firmware version.
        
    *   In some cases, such as with standard release versions, WizarView might not generate a patch, requiring a full firmware update instead.
        
    
*   Procedure: Request the vendor to set up the target firmware. Then configure this firmware in TMS under ‘Application -> Firmware submenu’.
    
*   Firmware list for patch
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252F9ORz9h2RqV2zhjOeXH7z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d78c85d-3d01-44a9-92fc-0f24b880cde8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3295c16e&sv=2)

*   Configure terminals and groups
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252F4GJol0AsuAQptqi4P1am%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8fc873de-273a-466f-a944-258b08d63a6d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89957b49&sv=2)

Note:

*   The choice of method depends on factors like terminal storage capacity, network connectivity, and the specific requirements of the terminal's current firmware version.
    
*   For all methods, ensure that you have reliable internet connectivity and that the terminal remains powered during the update process to prevent any interruptions or firmware corruption.
    

[PreviousApply RMA Maintenance Accountchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/apply-rma-maintenance-account)
[NextPush APK to Specific Devicechevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apk-to-specific-device)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Update with Full Firmware Package](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/update-firmware-remotely#update-with-full-firmware-package)
    
*   [Update with Specific Firmware Patch Package](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/update-firmware-remotely#update-with-specific-firmware-patch-package)

# Manage APK Prompt Installation | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#overview)

Overview

For kiosk terminals or similar devices, there may be a need to decide when to install an APK. This process involves configuring the APK in TMS for prompt installation mode. This setup allows the customer's APK to receive a notification when the download is complete and then instruct the Wizarview agent to proceed with the installation.

Required Version: Ensure the Wizarview agent version is greater than 5.3.39 for this functionality to work effectively.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#receive-download)

Receive download

Copy

     Receive the broadcast, action：android.intent.action.TMS_DOWNLOADED   extra value name: apk_notify_info  type: JSONArray, for example: [{"appId":19068,"newVersion":1,"newVersionName":"1.0","packageName":"com.liqi.myapp20210324"}]

*   Register broadcast
    

Copy

      <receiver
    	android:name=".receiver.ApkDownloadedReceiver">
        <intent-filter>
            <action android:name="android.intent.action.TMS_DOWNLOADED" />
        </intent-filter>
    </receiver>

*   Extends class of the BroadcastReceiver
    

Copy

        String apk_notify_info = intent.getStringExtra("apk_notify_info");

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#notice-to-install)

Notice to install

Copy

     Send broadcast to install, action: android.intent.action.TMS_INSTALL  extra value name: apk_start_install_notify_info type: JSONArray, for example: [{"appId":19068,"newVersion":1,"newVersionName":"1.0","packageName":"com.liqi.myapp20210324"}]

Copy

        Intent intent = new Intent();
        intent.putExtra("apk_start_install_notify_info", JSON.toJSONString(apkNotifyInfos));
        intent.setAction("android.intent.action.TMS_INSTALL");
        context.sendBroadcast(intent);

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#apknotifyinfo-class)

ApkNotifyInfo class

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#considerations)

Considerations

*   This configuration is particularly useful for scenarios where installations need to be managed without interrupting the terminal's primary functions.
    
*   Ensure that the APK and TMS settings are correctly aligned to avoid installation delays or failures.
    
*   The configuration process might vary slightly based on the version of your TMS and the specific type of terminal you are using. Always refer to the latest documentation for your TMS version for the most accurate guidance.
    

[PreviousSet Agent Working Modechevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/set-agent-working-mode)
[NextNetwork Control in Agentchevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/network-control-in-agent)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Overview](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#overview)
    
*   [Receive download](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#receive-download)
    
*   [Notice to install](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#notice-to-install)
    
*   [ApkNotifyInfo class](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#apknotifyinfo-class)
    
*   [Considerations](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation#considerations)
    

Copy

       class ApkNotifyInfo {
            private int appId;
            private String packageName;
            private long newVersion;
            private String newVersionName;
    
            public ApkNotifyInfo() {
            }
    
            public ApkNotifyInfo(int appId, String packageName, long newVersion, String newVersionName) {
                this.appId = appId;
                this.packageName = packageName;
                this.newVersion = newVersion;
                this.newVersionName = newVersionName;
            }
    
            public int getAppId() {
                return appId;
            }
    
            public void setAppId(int appId) {
                this.appId = appId;
            }
    
            public String getPackageName() {
                return packageName;
            }
    
            public void setPackageName(String packageName) {
                this.packageName = packageName;
            }
    
            public long getNewVersion() {
                return newVersion;
            }
    
            public void setNewVersion(long newVersion) {
                this.newVersion = newVersion;
            }
    
            public String getNewVersionName() {
                return newVersionName;
            }
    
            public void setNewVersionName(String newVersionName) {
                this.newVersionName = newVersionName;
            }
    }

# Push Apps Using Tags | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apps-using-tags#overview)

Overview

Wizarview manages terminals in groups, making it easy to configure the same apps for all terminals within a single group. However, to configure apps for terminals across different groups, the use of Tags is essential. Tags offer an additional dimension for managing terminal apps for varied purposes, allowing for cross-group configurations.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apps-using-tags#steps-to-push-apps-using-tags)

Steps to Push Apps Using Tags

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apps-using-tags#create-tag)

Create Tag

Click Terminal>Terminal Tag, it will display the Tag list, click icon button Add

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FMft210VErLt2usWnyTFU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc73fcb45-dae6-4b11-941e-ba81efbcd899&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66e93691&sv=2)

, then create new tag for different requirements, for example we can create 3 tags, gym, catering, loyalty:

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FQXxFVEKeCFyQT0eBKAEB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D181a534e-bdfb-43ad-a4e6-dbb69e6e6fc3&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c7052085&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FkRpIyQ54IkD3eJunvPq8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf98f182-500a-44b8-849a-7d89d02154ef&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83cd0d4b&sv=2)![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FUVlXN3cQQTqrrRLjXbZO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5d9008a-c66e-4644-86d0-2011e1276628&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=24fda0a8&sv=2)

Configure Tag

Click icon button Config

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FAjUEM7Uw7uLYYRiwuIc3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D696f4c4a-5e4c-4c6b-85a6-2722113210df&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b64645e&sv=2)

, it will display Tag Configure window.

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FfSrJufWyopaFxw4xmZeb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff245c67-61aa-4da7-b402-29f92a229fa8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=80e53d19&sv=2)

In the bottom Terminal List, choose terminals, perhaps the terminals are in different groups, for example terminals in East City group, North City group, click Configure button in the bottom, then they can configure the same tag.

Click Config Application tab, then configure Apps for the tag

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FkkulUkXZhFGDHU8bAIIm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6fe53d87-1d59-4d76-8354-a9e3a9288995&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81565f19&sv=2)

In the bottom Application List, choose application, then click Configure button, you can configure many apps for the tag. After above two steps, the tag has configured successfully.

If you want batch configure terminals, you can click Batch Config Terminal tab, input SNs as requirement. Here is the batch config page:

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FxAfQefSKftEipPmqv0Oa%252F1714013440547.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D052080c6-8831-4ca1-9849-c95f6218d21e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a06be72b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apps-using-tags#push-tag)

Push Tag

Choose the tag in Tag list, click Push Apps, it will push immediately.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apps-using-tags#monitor-the-tag-download-status)

Monitor the Tag download status

Choose Monitor>Download log, if will display the terminals which downloaded applications configured in the tag. And if you want to search one application, you should input the application name in Application input area, click Search button, if will display which terminals downloaded the application

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FslgI1Iddk72Lv9T1cmCK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd512fcaa-2c5b-428c-88e6-9833f0988b17&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6f31ebb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apps-using-tags#considerations)

Considerations

*   Cross-Group Management: Utilizing tags effectively allows for more flexible and targeted app deployment across various groups.
    
*   Tag Consistency: Ensure tags are consistently applied across the terminals for accurate app deployment.
    
*   This method is particularly useful when you need to target a specific subset of terminals that do not fall under a single group but share common characteristics or requirements denoted by the tags.

# Deploy AID/CAPK via TMS | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/deploy-aid-capk-via-tms#overview)

Overview

This guide provides a detailed process for adding, updating, and deploying AID and CAPK as part of the payment parameters in TMS. Specifically tailored for payment parameter configurations, the following steps are primarily focused on AID. It's important to note that the procedure for CAPK follows a similar pattern, ensuring a cohesive and efficient management experience within TMS environment.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/deploy-aid-capk-via-tms#steps)

Steps

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/deploy-aid-capk-via-tms#accessing-ald-profile-and-data)

Accessing AlD Profile & Data

1.  Navigate to Parameters > AlD Profile & AlD Data. This will lead you to the AlD Profle & AlD Data page.
    

![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252F31mB4CS2xakB4Hgfs24A%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D206ee01e-ba3a-458e-ac50-dc25ed3f1daf&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28a77591&sv=2)

**Adding AlD Data**

1.  Select the AlD Data tab and click the Add icon. This opens the AlD Data page.![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FPeK6IhFO64IEUZOGVtoA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3fcf7a10-c141-43e1-bd94-3766a8019c35&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=15a4fe06&sv=2)
    
2.  After entering necessary information, click the Commit button to create the AlD Data.
    

**Creating AlD Profile**

1.  Switch to the AlD Profile tab and click the Add icon, leading to the AlD Profile page. ![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252Fgj3ooMQIHTfEA22Xkjle%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99f89d9b-34ff-4478-a9e2-2d7e69165011&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72d6be20&sv=2)
    
2.  Fill in the required details and click the Commit button to create the AlD Profile.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/deploy-aid-capk-via-tms#setting-up-prototype)

Setting Up Prototype

1.  Go to Parameters > ProtoType. This takes you to the ProtoType page.![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FYnyYLnraCkGgnr92b3fN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D111e07d5-9c35-407c-b966-12cdcd6acd5d&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e351128&sv=2)
    
2.  Click the Add icon, fill in details on the Add ProtoType page, and commit the changes. The sample file , please download [herearrow-up-right](https://ftp.wizarpos.com/advanceSDK/basicpaymentpramtemplate.xml)
    .
    
    ![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FQkiluhKzDdpoVB4Geu7k%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D812bc3c1-fec3-4849-82fd-90ea2a0f76d8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7efc1894&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/deploy-aid-capk-via-tms#template-and-profile-configuration)

Template & Profile Configuration

1.  Select Parameters > Template & Profile to access the Template List page.![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FlQ4EXcS5awEsGdB67Akh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db65462aa-7b5b-448e-a070-5a8dff8f61a4&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2d60d46&sv=2)
    
2.  To add a template, click the Add icon and enter details on the Add Template page. Commit to create the template![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FQYYT8W7KD1UugJegmDGt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6c4de57-5e4a-4aa4-ae54-9953b605b0ff&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aa6f83e4&sv=2)
    
3.  Configure the template by selecting it and clicking the Configure icon. Commit the changes after configuration![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FPd3A5uxwWz1C3jBu7RNn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc713c5ec-e796-451b-9850-de38009ed448&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1846091&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/deploy-aid-capk-via-tms#managing-terminal-payment-parameters)

Managing Terminal Payment Parameters

1.  Navigate to Parameters > Terminal Payment Parameter for the parameter list.
    
2.  To add a payment parameter, click the Add icon and enter details on the respective page. Commit to create the parameter![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252F2xOs221KSWlEp3s7PJQB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2259c187-7281-4e0a-a4f6-166cd0b6e5bc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20f43c27&sv=2)
    
3.  To modify a payment parameter, select it, make changes (including selecting the correct AlD orCAPK), and commit the modifications![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FdN787p5P9a1HsnkpIBdF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b8bf534-209c-4f9e-bc30-c06bbd0c1c8a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e1f0f3f&sv=2)
    
4.  Deploy the parameter by clicking the Deploy Parameter button.![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FA5tzZ1PENf1vWTGKfOoV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbfaf0fdc-d52e-4869-856e-c4ebb4c4a420&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=802b2da0&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/deploy-aid-capk-via-tms#reviewing-deployed-payment-parameters)

Reviewing Deployed Payment Parameters

1.  To view deployed parameters, select Parameters > Deployed Payment Parameter![](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3254882245-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTv6FkzHXX8QyxZpeenq6%252Fuploads%252FcpIVuNKLsOJkEqzwWWKI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e2740e7-682d-40e4-b36f-964cda6046f0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8675c356&sv=2)

# Network Control in Agent | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/network-control-in-agent#prerequisite)

Prerequisite

*   Ensure that the Wizarview agent version on the device is greater than 5.3.39 to use this feature.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/network-control-in-agent#steps-to-control-network-usage)

Steps to Control Network Usage

*   Prepare the Broadcast Intent:
    
    *   You will need to send a broadcast intent to control the network usage of the Wizarview agent.
        
    *   The action for the intent should be set to: 'android.intent.action.NET\_USE\_CONTROL'.
        
    
*   Set the Extra Value:
    
    *   Along with the action, you need to include an extra value in the broadcast.
        
    *   The extra value should have the name 'net\_use\_control\_flag'.
        
    *   The value for this should be either 'enable' or 'disable', depending on whether you want to activate or deactivate the network usage.
        
    
*   Enable
    

Copy

      Intent enableIntent = new Intent();
      enableIntent.putExtra("net_use_control_flag", "enable");
      enableIntent.setAction("android.intent.action.NET_USE_CONTROL");
      getApplicationContext().sendBroadcast(enableIntent);

*   Disable
    

Copy

      Intent disableIntent = new Intent();
      disableIntent.putExtra("net_use_control_flag", "disable");
      disableIntent.setAction("android.intent.action.NET_USE_CONTROL");
      getApplicationContext().sendBroadcast(disableIntent);

Note:

*   It's important to correctly implement this broadcast mechanism, as incorrect usage could lead to unintended behaviors in the Wizarview agent's network management.
    
*   This feature is particularly useful for customers who need precise control over their device's network activities for efficiency or security reasons.
    

[PreviousManage APK Prompt Installationchevron-left](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/manage-apk-prompt-installation)
[NextPush Apps Using Tagschevron-right](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/push-apps-using-tags)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Prerequisite](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/network-control-in-agent#prerequisite)
    
*   [Steps to Control Network Usage](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/tms-wizarview/network-control-in-agent#steps-to-control-network-usage)
