# Display Full-Screen API | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/display-full-screen-api#overview)

Overview

This guide explains how to use specific system APIs to hide the status bar and navigation bar, enabling a full-screen display on Android devices.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/display-full-screen-api#important-considerations)

Important Considerations

Be aware that using these APIs affects the entire system, not just your application. When you hide the status bar or navigation bar, it remains hidden across all system interfaces and applications.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/display-full-screen-api#permission)

Permission

Copy

     android.permission.CLOUDPOS_HIDE_STATUS_BAR

The application declares permissions in the manifest.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/display-full-screen-api#api-overview)

API Overview

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/display-full-screen-api#hide-or-show-status-navigation-bar-using-hidebars)

Hide or show status/navigation bar using HideBars

Copy

    void hideBars(int state)

Set status bar and navigation bar state.

Parameters

state

1 - hide status bar, 2 - hide navigation bar, 3 - hide both, 0 - show both. _In device without navigation bar, set 2 and 3 will throw IllegalArgumentException._ 11 - Automatically hide the status bar globally (can be pulled down), 12 - Automatically hide the navigation bar globally (can be pulled up), 13 - Automatically hide all globally (can be pulled down and up), 22 - Globally hide the status bar and automatically hide the navigation bar (can be pulled up), 23 - Automatically hide the status bar globally (can be pulled down) and hide the navigation bar

Here are some code snippets:

Copy

    //hideBars:
    Object service = getSystemService("statusbar");
    Class statusBarManager = Class.forName("android.app.StatusBarManager");
    Method method = statusBarManager.getMethod("hideBars", int.class);
    method.invoke(service, 3);

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/display-full-screen-api#getbarsvisibility)

GetBarsVisibility

Get the state of the status bar and navigation bar.

Returns

int

the result , 1 : hide status bar, 2 : hide navigation bar, 3: hide both, 0: show both. In device without navigation bar, set 2 and 3 will throw IllegalArgumentException.

Here are some code snippets:

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/display-full-screen-api#download)

Please download the [source demoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/SmartPOSSamples/StatusBarDemo.git)
.

# Learn Kiosk Mode | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/learn-kiosk-mode#overview-of-android-kiosk-mode)

Overview of Android Kiosk Mode

Android kiosk mode is a specialized mode designed for public-use devices. It is commonly utilized in self-service kiosks, display devices, and similar applications in commercial and educational settings. In this mode, user access is limited to specific apps and features, and the ability to alter system settings or install new apps is restricted.

*   Key Features of Kiosk Mode:
    
    *   Restricted User Behavior: You can limit actions like changing screen brightness, adjusting volume, accessing the notification bar, and using physical buttons.
        
    *   Control Over App Lifecycle: Programmatically manage app operations, including auto-restarting apps upon exit and preventing users from switching to other apps.
        
    
*   Purpose of Kiosk Mode: Kiosk mode is instrumental in maintaining the security and controlled use of public devices, ensuring they operate within predefined limits.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/learn-kiosk-mode#enabling-kiosk-mode-by-using-android-native-methods)

Enabling Kiosk Mode by using Android native methods

Please refero to [Lock task modearrow-up-right](https://developer.android.com/work/dpc/dedicated-devices/lock-task-mode#java)

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/learn-kiosk-mode#download)

Download

**Demo**

We have created a simple demo of Kiosk mode, exclusively using Android APIs. Please note that this demo is intended for use on devices running Android 12 and above. When used on devices with Android versions below 12, a confirmation popup will appear.

Please download the [kiosk demoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/SmartPOSSamples/KioskMode)

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/learn-kiosk-mode#enabling-kiosk-mode-below-android-12-by-using-wizarpos-aidl-method)

Enabling Kiosk Mode below Android 12 by using WizarPOS AIDL method

*   Use of AIDL Interface: Android kiosk mode can be enabled through the Application Interface Definition Language (AIDL) provided by the system.
    
*   Import Required Service: Utilize the 'wizarviewagentassistant' service.
    
*   Service Initialization: When initiating the service, use 'com.wizarpos.wizarviewagentassistant' as the package name and 'com.wizarpos.wizarviewagentassistant.SystemExtApiService' as the class name.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/learn-kiosk-mode#required-permissions)

Required Permissions

The application declares the following permissions in the manifest：

API Overview

**startLockTaskMode**

Request to put this activity in a mode where the user is locked to a restricted set of applications.

Parameters

taskId

int: task id.

Returns

boolean

true:success ; false: failed;

# Update Terminal Time | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-terminal-time#automatic-update-via-wi-fi)

Automatic Update via Wi-Fi

*   When the Wi-Fi connection is enabled, the date and time will automatically update.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-terminal-time#manual-update)

Manual Update

*   Go to: Settings > Date & Time.
    
*   Disable "Automatic time zone" and "Automatic date & time".
    
*   Manually set the date and time as needed.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-terminal-time#update-via-api)

Update via API

*   Utilize the Android system clock method to change the system time programmatically.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-terminal-time#required-permissions)

Required Permissions

*   To use the API method, include the following permission in your application's manifest: **'android.permission.CLOUDPOS\_SETTIME**'.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-terminal-time#accessing-demo-source)

Accessing Demo Source

*   To understand the implementation details, please download the [complete project demoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/SmartPOSSamples/SetTimeDemo)
    .
    

Copy

    public static void setDateTime(int year, int month, int day, int hour, int minute) throws IOException, InterruptedException {
    
            Calendar c = Calendar.getInstance();
            c.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
            c.set(Calendar.MONTH, month-1);
            c.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
            c.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
            c.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minute);
    
            long when = c.getTimeInMillis();
            if (when / 1000 < Integer.MAX_VALUE) {
                SystemClock.setCurrentTimeMillis(when);
            }
            long now = Calendar.getInstance().getTimeInMillis();
            //Log.d(TAG, "set tm="+when + ", now tm="+now);
    
            if(now - when > 1000)
                throw new IOException("failed to set Date.");
    
        }

# Get Wifi Mac | CloudPOS SDK

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/get-wifi-mac#permission)

Permission

The application declares the following permissions in the manifest：

Copy

     android.permission.WIFI

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/get-wifi-mac#api-overview)

API Overview

Copy

    byte[] getWifiMac();

Get Mac of Wifi.

Returns

byte\[\]

Mac array.

**Resource Download**

*   Refer to the cloudpos apidemo - [demoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/SmartPOSSamples/APIDemoForAar.git)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/get-wifi-mac#snippet-code)

Snippet code

Copy

    private ISystemDevice device;
    if (device == null) {
      device = POSTerminalAdvance.getInstance().getSystemDevice();
    }
    device.open(context);
    device.getNetworkManager().open(context);
    device.getNetworkManager().getWifiManager().open(context);
    byte[] wifiMacByte = device.getNetworkManager().getWifiManager().getWifiMac();
    device.getNetworkManager().getWifiManager().close();
    device.getNetworkManager().close();
    device.close();

**Resource Download**

*   Refer to the cloudpos apidemo - [demoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/SmartPOSSamples/APIDemoForAar.git)

# Update Role Passwords API | CloudPOS SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-role-passwords-api#required-permissions)

Required Permissions

*   Include the following permissions in your application's manifest:
    
    *   'android.permission.USER\_PWD': permission for isUserPwd.
        
    *   'android.permission.USER\_PWD\_MODIFY': permission for forceModifyUserPwd, enableUserLogin.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-role-passwords-api#api-functions)

API Functions

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-role-passwords-api#verifyuserpwd)

verifyUserPwd

Copy

    boolean verifyUserPwd(String pwd);

Checks if the provided string ('pwd') is the current user password.

Parameters

pwd

the user role password. It can not be null

Returns

boolean

a boolean representation of the result.

true if success. false if failure.

#### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-role-passwords-api#forcemodifyuserpwd)

forceModifyUserPwd

Copy

    boolean forceModifyUserPwd(String newPwd);

Modifies the user role password to the new password ('newPwd').

Parameters

newPwd

the new user role password. It can not be null

Returns

boolean

a boolean representation of the result.

true if success. false if failure.

setUserLoginMode

Enables or disables user role login based on the boolean value ('enable').

Parameters

eneable

for the user login setting, a boolean value is used: true enables user login, while false disables it.

Returns

boolean

a boolean representation of the result.

true if success. false if failure.

isUserLoginMode

Check whether enable user role login mode.

Returns

boolean

a boolean representation of the result.

true if enable. false if disable.

### 

[hashtag](https://smartpossdk.gitbook.io/cloudpossdk/faq/advance-sdk/update-role-passwords-api#undefined)

isUserLoggedIn

Check whether the user logged in.

Returns

boolean

a boolean representation of the result.

true if logged in. false if not.

**Resource Download**

*   Refer to the cloudpos apidemo - [demoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/SmartPOSSamples/APIDemoForAar.git)
    .
